2.即使钱赚够了，也很不舍得花费时间亲手做那么多流程（比如某期视频中的，自己种玉米，摘玉米，做玉米面）。时间宁愿花在娱乐影音和陪喜欢/所爱之人消遣时光。

Her life comes through the hard time, deprived from schooling and to be a DJ working at the bar for small money when she was young. Her Daddy's death makes her thinking of her grandmother who lives alone in the countryside, as recalls of responsibility, however she comes back to her hometown. Primarily, she made the videos to promote the products that she opened on internet. In reality, she was nothing for a couple of years until a big-time name distributor helped her to be well known sellers. In difference with other online sellers in China on YouTube, what her videos present are not only the matters of food making, but also content many aspects of sense of beauty and creativity which exhibits the traditions and spirit of the ancient China. It is in benefit of the audiences in the world are able to know that the life in the countryside was used to be, and the tenacity and intelligence of Chinese people how to survive. I pray for Ziqi and her lovely grandmother, Amen!

Translation from Chinese to English:

黄豆 Soybeans
生长 Growing up
秋分 Autumn equinox 
晒干 Dry in the sun
寒露 Cold dew(one of the Chinese solar terms)
存储 Store
浸泡至发胀 Soak the soybeans in the water until they become swelled 
小麦粉 Wheat flour
摊凉 Spread them out and cool them down 
制曲 Make Koji(a kind of mold used to make soybean into soy sauce)
盐水搅匀 Mix some salt with water
日晒半年左右 Put the crockery in the sun for about half a year
夜露 Night dew
二零一九秋分 The autumn equinox of 2019
加山泉回浸一日 Put some  mountain spring in for one more day
暴晒提纯 Put the crockery in the sun again and make it more purified
二零一九小雪 The Light Snow (one of the Chinese solar terms) of 2019
熬煮沸腾 Cook it until it boils out
放凉装罐 Cool it down and put it in a crockery 
手工酱油 Handmade soy sauce

Liang Shan's translation:


0:08 黄豆(Huang Dou): Soybean

 生长(Sheng Zhang): Grow

 秋分(Qiu Fen): The September equinox (solar terms)

 晾干(Liang Gan): Air-dry

 寒露(Han Lu) (solar terms)

 存储(Cun Chu): Storage


 浸泡至发胀(Jin Pao Zhi Fa Zhang): Soak till swelled

 小麦粉(Xiao Mai Fen): Wheat flour

 摊凉(Tan Liang): Cooling

 制曲(Zhi Qu): Koji

 盐水搅匀(Yan Shui Jiao Yun): Blending with brine

 日晒半年左右(Ri Shai Ban Nian Zuo You): Sun exposure for around half a year

 期间每日翻晒(Qi Jian Mei Ri Fan Shai): Stir and sun each day during the time

 夜露(Ye Lu): Night dew

 二零一九秋分(Er Ling Yi Jiu  Qiu Fen): 2019 September equinox (solar terms)


 加山泉回浸一日(Jia Shan Quan Hui Jin Yi Ri): Soak with spring water for an extra day

 暴晒提纯(Pu Shai Ti Chun): Sun exposure for fining

 二零一九小雪(Er Ling Yi Jiu  Xiao Xue): 2019 Xiaoxue (solar terms)

记得早先少年时

Remember the old days

大家诚诚恳恳

when everyone was sincere

说一句 是一句

one's word is one's bond

清早上火车站

The dawn of the train station


the dark street with no sign of pedestrian

卖豆浆的小店冒着热气

and the steam from the soy-milk stall

从前的日色变得慢

The nighfalls used to come late in the past

车，马，邮件都慢

Everything was slow, the bike, the horse, and the post


a lifetime was all but enough to be in love with one

从前的锁也好看

The old-school lock was beautiful


and the key exquisite looking

你锁了 人家就懂了

once locked, the others understood

Shared recipe for the “卤肉&蛋” (Soy Sauce Pork & Egg) which is easier for non-Chinese cookers: 1.5 KG pork rib (more friendly for beginners than pork belly,  remember to slice with one or two bones on each piece), 8~12  boiled eggs (even more delicious than meat after cooking, two eggs are not enough at all),  80 ml sweet soy sauce （老抽，show these two strange Chinese characters to the local Chinese supermarket or try to find a Japanese version in a large supermaket）, 80 ml salty soy sauce （生抽，same to the sweet soy sauce）, Chinese spice combo (1. 桂皮, dried cinnamon bark 10g, 2. 八角, dried star anise 10g, 3. 香叶, dried bay leaf 10g), 150g sliced ginger, 2L beer (yes, use beer instead of water makes it nicer, 500ml*4 or 330ml*6). Throw everything into the pot and stew for 2h+ with slow fire. Let's repeat: rib, egg, soy sauce, spice, ginger, beer. That's all, no salt or butter or anything else. This is a beginner recipe for 2~3 persons, you can share it with your family/roommate or store it in the fridge to enjoy it yourself.

English Translation
Ziqi Li's attitude toward life and way of life are inspiring to me. I tried to translate the Chinese words put on the screen and said by Ziqi into English. Frankly, even though I was born in Sichuan where she is currently living, I cannot figure out some of the words she said in the video.  The translation is given as follows alongside the corresponding Chinese.  Hope it will be of some help for those fans of Ziqi who do not understand Chinese or the Sichuan dialect she says.
黄豆 /soybean
生长 /Growing
秋分 /The autumnal equinox
寒露 /Cold dew (17th solar term, time for autumn harvest, around early October)
存储 /Storing
浸泡至发胀/Soaking beans until they swell
小麦粉 /Wheat flour
摊凉 /Spreading beans till they cool down
制曲 /Making Koji (starter)
盐水搅拌 /Stirring in saltwater
日晒半年左右 /Exposing in the sun for about 1/2 year
期间每日翻晒 /During this time, stirring and turning daily
夜露 /Exposing in night
加山泉水浸泡一日 /Adding fountain water and soaking for one day
暴晒提纯 /Exposing under the sun and purifying
2019 小雪/Lesser snow 2019 (20st solar term, around late November)

熬煮沸腾 /Stewing until it boils

放凉装罐 /Cooling it down and canning
手工酱/Handmade soy sauce
姜葱蒜糖 辣椒  水 醋 /Ginger, green onion, garlic, sugar; pepper; water, vinegar
加适量酱油腌制一日 /Adding the right amount of soy sauce and pickling for one day
姜葱蒜 料酒 /Ginger, green onion, garlic; cooking wine
酱油 /Soy sauce
腌制过夜 /Pickling over the night
李:我觉得可以做窑鸡，婆婆 /Li: I think we can cook a Yaoji (chicken baked in the sauce when wrapped with vegetable leaves)
李:哇塞/wow,好久没吃过了哦/Li: Wow, it's a long time since my last chance of eating it.
李:我出去捡两个泥巴，等我一会儿/Li: I am going to get some clay lumps. Wait for me.
五花肉焯水 /Stewing streaky pork for a little while
洋葱 蒜  煸干/Red onion, garlic; Dry-frying
炒糖色 /Stir-frying until a yellowish color appears
香菇丁 洋葱 蒜 /Diced mushroom, red onion, garlic

She use the word ginger whereas it is more famous for the special vinegar.This dish is popularly consumed during confinement month as it is believed to expel dampness, preventing aches and pains when mommies grow to middle age.  Everything is consumed and hard boiled eggs topped up as the dish can be re-heated for several days.

李子柒 she was born in Sichuan (province) Mianyang in July 6 of 1990, her mom left the poor family when she was very little; she was treated badly by her step-mother at six when her father away from home. Then she became an orphan living with her grand-parents when her father died in an accident. She became a middle school drop-off and left the countryside at the age of 14 due to the poor farmer.  She went to Shenzhen since then and worked as waitress or a bar DJ for 8 years (300-3000 RMB/mo, about US $50-500/mo until her grandpa passed away in 2012, who is a chef for  countryside-dinner-party, such as for wedding and funeral. That's why most of her videos are related to Chinese countryside cooking. Now her video income on YouTube alone exceeds $200k/yr. BTW, any videos before June of 2017 were made by herself. Some videos on YouTube were made by a three-person team (li, assistant and photographer).In Chinese her name spelling as: li  (lee), ziqi  (zeechee, 'i' pronounced 'ee' most likely). I know her childhood story by other Chinese  videos and interviews in recent two years. She doesn't have an English name, and this official youtube account  (as her real name in Chinese) is operated by her affiliates in China (via VPN, I believe)Li (ziqi) was not engaged so far since she was engaging the countryside cooking media. During  several interviews in China, she mentioned her home-making vedio was started  by her younger brother, who played lots of self-vedio-shooting on cellphone. Though we have never seen her brother in vedios  (maybe her half-brother or from her step-mother), she did emphasize the initiative, encouraging and enthusiasm from her brother.

李子柒 she was born in Sichuan (province) Mianyang in July 6 of 1990, her mom left the poor family when she was very little; she was treated badly by her step-mother at six when her father away from home. Then she became an orphan living with her grand-parents when her father died in an accident. She became a middle school drop-off and left the countryside at the age of 14 due to the poor farmer.  She went to Shenzhen since then and worked as waitress or a bar DJ for 8 years (300-3000 RMB/mo, about US $50-500/mo until her grandpa passed away in 2012, who is a chef for  countryside-dinner-party, such as for wedding and funeral. That's why most of her videos are related to Chinese countryside cooking. Now her video income on YouTube alone exceeds $200k/yr. BTW, any videos before June of 2017 were made by herself. Some videos on YouTube were made by a three-person team (li, assistant and photographer).In Chinese her name spelling as: li  (lee), ziqi  (zeechee, 'i' pronounced 'ee' most likely). I know her childhood story by other Chinese  videos and interviews in recent two years. She doesn't have an English name, and this official youtube account  (as her real name in Chinese) is operated by her affiliates in China (via VPN, I believe)Li (ziqi) was not engaged so far since she was engaging the countryside cooking media. During  several interviews in China, she mentioned her home-making vedio was started  by her younger brother, who played lots of self-vedio-shooting on cellphone. Though we have never seen her brother in vedios  (maybe her half-brother or from her step-mother), she did emphasize the initiative, encouraging and enthusiasm from her brother.

The following content was wrote by Li Ziq in Chinese ：-----（I saw this video last night on weibo，i know she will post on YouTube soon，so i translate them last night ：））I heard the  Magnoliae flower should send to someone you loveI guess i must love you guys very much....(shy~~)I am so satisfied nowI would pretentiously ride a horse and then pretentiously collect the flowers  （she's mocking herself )I always want to capture a scene when I am riding a horse----- (I think she might also want a sword to be attached on the side of her horse ：) ，it creates an elegant，valiant and heroic image of women….probably like people say they wanna be a Knight in western culture：P)But never got a chanceAfter finish that “Scholar's four jewels”video，I had a rest ….for a while.I borrowed uncle Peng‘s horse “HeiWa”to went for a walk for like a half day.It is the Magnoliae flower blossoming season nowtook a long way to get a lot of these flowers from grandpa Liu ----（He is not her real grandpa，Chinese call elder male “grandpa” sometimes，BTW，her real grandpa passed away when she was in 5th grade）Magnoliae flower can be used for medicineIt is the right time to have them ！(eat them)Every  Magnoliae flower are 10 months of pregnancyJune in each year ，it breeds buds，March or April in every coming year ，it will blossomEvery  Magnoliae buds picked in autumn can be use for making medicine and teaother content are about how she used different part of those flowers to make tea ，sauce，cake，egg pie ，snacks….etc------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------PS：Did anyone notice that horse through a path with flowers on the ground ？That scene reminds me of two Chinese poem have that scene “踏花归去马蹄香” Nobody knows who wrote this poem ，other poet use this sentence in their poemOne is about a warrior fight for protecting his country“几年鏖战历沙场，汗马功高孰可量？四海狼烟今已熄，踏花归去马蹄香 ”It means “After years of bloodletting on the killing fields, how does one even begin measure a warhorse's worth? Now that the war beacons are finally extinguished, the hooves of my horse has turned fragrant, as we tread on flowers on the way home. ”------Song dynastyAnother is about spring outing“拂石坐来衣带冷，踏花归去马蹄香” which means “The spring is coming，I went out for a walk ，I was sitting on a rock when I am tired ，the cold air still can go through my light clothes ，the hooves of my horse has turned fragrant, as we tread on flowers on the way home ”-----Tang dynastyAnother interesting story is also about this poem，about this scene .One of emperor from North Song dynasty really love painting, He used to hold a exam between painters ，How to paint “踏花归去马蹄香 ”Many people don’t know how to paint that scene ,they painted flowers on the path ,but one painter ,he didn’t paint any flower but a horse with butterflies flying around the horseshoe .And the emperor really like his painting at that time-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------Last video，some people ask if I can explain all her videos ，Since She can’t speak English，as one of her big fan ，I will just try with my Chinglish ：PI believe many Chinese know much much better English than me will do the job somedayBecause most of her titles and contents ，she wrote in a poetic way，they are really beautiful and romantic in Chinese ,I hope someone will translate all those into better English. thanksBTW,i think youtube is removing her views ，i just saw 467 views 810 likes 132comments in 2 minutes after she post this video， this video already got 12.84 million views on weibo （Chinese Twitter） in 22 hours ，each her video can got average 40 million views on weibolast video，it got 7707 comments ，but only 1.6 million views ，it is kind of weird ,maybe i am wrong ,Nevermind ：）

This is the real Mulan 木兰, Magnolia liliiflora, one of the oldest flowering plants on earth. It is native to China and is now planted all over the world. However, the deep purple color of Mulan can only be seen in Yunnan, China. Magnolia liliiflora flowers are not able to keep pure deep purple color in other places, they turned to light purple to white color when moved to the other countries.

The “four treasures of the study”一writing brush, ink stick, ink slab and paper―are writing tools with a long cultural tradition and unique artistic style created by the ancestors of the Chinese nation. They have played an important role in recording Chinese history, popularizing various cultures, and promoting the development of Chinese calligraphic and pointing art over thousands of years.Today, they are duplicated by a beautiful, and ingenuity，and angelic young girl by a pairs of weak slender, and delicate hands, with the hard working project for a year and half, finally completing a traditional Chinese landscape painting through her entire project ! Unbelievable!
每一个动作都是那么的娴熟, 绝对是认真学过专业制作手法和大量练习的结果, 根本不是某些网红随便做做动作摆拍能比的.

Translation and Introduction:Brush pen, ink stick, paper and inkstone (笔 墨 纸 砚) aka Four Treasures in Study Room of ancient China. Each of them have their own complex technological processes to be finished.Miss Li started to make ink in autumn 2017, and waited one yr above (dry and no shape). In autumn 2018, ink was shaped into sticks and chopped purple (and other types of) bamboos to dry and waited until spring 2019 (make it straight and hard). The head of these two pens are made by goat fur and rabbit fur respectively.In autumn 2017, she started to make paper. Trees were peeled and boiled (10 hours above ) with plant ash.In spring 2019, she made inkstone (for rubbing ink), and drew a Chinese painting (bamboo). And she went to Malaysia introduced to people 4 treasures in study room.Among these four, papermaking tech is one of the four ancient inventions in China (other 3: compass, gunpowder, printing )Besides, calligraphy is an art expression ever since the born of Chinese characters and has developed five traditional genres.Hope you enjoy.

李子柒 she was born in Sichuan province in July 6 of 1990, her mom left the poor family when she was very little; she was treated badly by her step-mother at six when her father away from home. Then she became an orphan living with her grand-parents when her father died in an accident. She became a middle school drop-off and left the countryside at the age of 14 due to the poor farmer.  She went to Shenzhen since then and worked as waitress or a bar DJ for 8 years (300-3000 RMB/mo, about US $50-500/mo until her grandpa passed away in 2012, who is a chef for  countryside-dinner-party, such as for wedding and funeral. That's why most of her videos are related to Chinese countryside cooking. Now her video income on YouTube alone exceeds $200k/yr. BTW, any videos before June of 2017 were made by herself. Some videos on YouTube were made by a three-person team (li, assistant and photographer).In Chinese her name spelling as: li  (lee), ziqi  (zeechee, 'i' pronounced 'ee' most likely). I know her childhood story by other Chinese  videos and interviews in recent two years. She doesn't have an English name, and this official youtube account  (as her real name in Chinese) is operated by her affiliates in China (via VPN, I believe)

My English isn't good but I really want to say this.For those who thinks she shouldn‘t push puppy like that.I want to say this is the different culture between China and other countries.In China is there a famous Taoist theory "天地不仁以万物为刍狗"，which means god has no mercy that he treats all creatures the same.In traditional Chinese culture we believe that all lifes are equal,ppl shouldn't treat some animals better than the other just because of personal preference,that will be unfair to the  we used to keep all the animals as “tools” rather than “pet”,some of us did have more preference to animals,such as dogs or cats,but this kind of "love" is just a love from a human to animals rather than to a family member(pet).We also keeped some animals just because we loved them,but in our minds is human always  matter how we love our hausanimals and no matter how much money we can pay for them,the fact is cruel---We keep animals because they are useful or they can bring us happy,they are used to satisfy us with certain purposes.Nowadays there are also "pet" in China because of the western influences but not all people receive the “new thought”.I hope we can understand the culture differences between each other and have less resentments.If u think my words indeed make sence,pls give a like to let more ppl see this.

just want to give some context to ppl who don't speak chinese on some of the dish names:1. pig is “zhu猪”, same pronunciation with "诸"，which means every6. 生财 (sheng1 cai2)means making money, and has the same pronunciation with the vegetable that she is using, which is "生菜(sheng1 cai4)". The vegetable is on a road, so it has a way. So making money has a way, or there is a way to become rich.7. chicken is "鸡ji 1", and chestnut is "栗li 4". Same tones with the characters that mean auspicious "吉ji 2" and "利li 4". It's "big chicken big chestnut", so it's lots of auspicious9. fish is "鱼yu2", same pronunciation with balance or extra "余yu2". Every year there is fish, so every year you have extra money or food10. man this is a tough one haha. "Only belongs to you" pronunciation is close to "smashed purple sweet potato and taro"

每次睡前看看子柒的视频，当晚的睡眠都能更沉稳。我觉得或许我们人类更适合这种与自然和睦相处的方式。国外工作了近7年的我，在这一年我非常想念我童年的小村庄。两年前回国曾直奔我的老家，虽然我们一家早已在我十岁的时候都到了一个大城市里生活。当我回到老家的时候，我以前跟着外婆洗过衣服的清澈河流，河水接近枯竭，颜色青到近乎黑，各种白色垃圾堆积发出腐臭。跟着小伙伴上山探险的整片竹林荡然无存，别说竹林，山也给削平了。从我家里望出去直至山脚 一望无际的各种庄稼不见了，变成了蓬养西瓜，变成了房屋，密密麻麻。下雨前我会跑出去捡跳出来的鱼的池塘，水草，游鸭，给死死的压在了水泥马路下。我知道我的童年再也找不回来了。我很羡慕子柒，她有回得去的家。也希望中国在追求发展的同时兼顾属于我们这个民族独有的东西。

Although I don't see this video has anything to do with KOREA or KIMCHI, I do want to clarify the following,We Chinese never call it KIMCHI.  We call it Paocai（泡菜）, and it is a very popular traditional dishes across whole China, especially in Sichuan Province, which is famous for its Sichuan Paocai, and almost every family there have their own secrete recipe.  since KIMCHI is quite similar with Paocai, we here in China call KIMCHI KOREAN PAOCAI(韩国泡菜), we never call them KIMCHI in Chinese.  so it should be google translation's fault who default translate the characters 泡菜(PAOCAI) into KIMCHI.

drunken crabs,醉蟹. using alcohol to preserve food，cook food is the very traditional way  in East China， especially in Zhe Jiang province , fisher man live a  long time on board ,they need a way to preserve their food , salt is not preferred cause fresh water is more  precious when you are on the ocean with no one to help , so Chinese fisher man use wine on almost everything they take on board, chicken,meat,pickles. they also use wine to preserve newly harvested fish,shell,shrimp,crabs,cause there is no fridge in old days.  i myself am from that province and my family still has some private wine-preserved dishes for holidays. we also use wine dross to make some weird but the most delicious food（in my view）,we use wet wine dross to wrap meat，chicken，fish，let them in fermentation for at least several months.  our ancestors  never waste anything from hard work.

子柒微博技术贴那个..视频里用的花是食用玫瑰，不是花店里卖的那那种月季切花。在月季玫瑰傻傻分不清楚的情况下不要跟着做嗷! ! !好了唠正事...玫瑰酱去年做过，不过去年用的大马士革，今年用的平阴玫瑰。做法都一样，天刚亮露水未干之时摘连夜盛开的玫瑰(所以我就没洗了，怕有灰尘的胖友就洗洗再晾干，不要有生水)花瓣+红糖-  :顿搓，  最后淋上一层蜂蜜在表面隔离空气就可以密封发酵了..至少三月以上，我后来做鲜花饼的玫瑰酱是去年拍视频做的那一罐，已经发酵一年...玫瑰米酒的做法跟传统米酒做法一样，不过多加了玫瑰花瓣，  泡米一夜，蒸八分熟，晾温拌入甜酒曲密封发酵，冬天时间久一点，夏天发酵快一点。装坛的时候我又多淋了一点凉白开进去~只是为了让它多出一点酒，不过这样发酵会慢一点，不加凉白开一般1到2天就发酵好了，加了要再多发酵个两三天。

Her dad passed away, when she was yelling at the mountains, she was asking 你还好吗 how were you. In Chinese. Translation: grandma said when I was still young I once got beaten by my father for crying for this dish. I can’t really remember but its what father left me. Its been 24years how were you on the other side? Forgive my horrible grammar and language, its basically what it means for those who don’t understand mandarin. 看到那个24年了，你还好吗......真的秒泪。君埋泉下泥销骨，我寄人间雪满头......

The translation:My nana said that it was the same season when I was a little girl, I used to ask for 刺龙苞 (the shoots and buds on the tree top in the video) with bad attitude. My dad beat me (for my stubbornness). (I guess it was not so convenient for her father collecting these buds) It was no use except making me crying loud. Finally my dad began to worry if he beat me too hard (to stop me crying), so he went to the mountain and brought me some. Honestly I don't remember it at all, neither the beat nor the taste of the bud dish. But my nana talks about it from time to time. Anyway, I made this dish in memory of him.  It has been 24 years (since he's gone), I think he's doing fine (in another world).

LaBa(腊八) Congee is a traditional Chinese food emerged in the very early stage of Chinese civilization. people use all kinds of beans that they harvested in autumn, game's meat to cook congee and share in the whole tribe, a ceremony to celebrate the end of the old year and beginning of new year. the day is the 8th，Dec in traditional Chinese calendar (it's not the same calendar been used all over the world )，腊 means the way that we preserve meat or the dried salty meat， 八 means 8th.  the flavor differ in different region of china, people in the south prefer sugared flavor. people in the north or some other place like salty taste. it's like a Chinese version Thanksgiving day. when the Buddism began to spread in China， that religion gave it their meaning, they choose it as a religious big day. In that day, monks will share LaBa Congee to believers for free.   you can still  have a taste of the congee for free in some Buddha temples nowadays.

The air dry in the La month (腊月), which is the last month in Chinese Calendar. And the dried meat is called La meat(腊肉). In my home town, there are about only 20 days good for making La meat every year. Traditional, people have to work according to the season. Now, with machines in the industry, La meat can be produced at any time during the year.

what she baked is traditional moon cake， Chinese eat moon cake at middle autumn festival day， the drink at the beginning of the clip is Osmanthus flavored wine.  In Chinese  myth, a goddess called 嫦娥 betrayed her god husband  后羿 after her husband shot down 9 Suns to save mortal people‘s lives，they are taken away their powers and could never return to heaven，a revenge from Sun's father, the almighty ruler of heaven. but another powerful god want to help this couple because they saved a lot of people‘s lives， so he gave them double doses of elixir to make them immortal again, if one of them drink both share, he(she) will have the power to return to heaven  , 嫦娥 missed heaven so much,  she swallowed both share of elixir when 后羿 fell asleep, her body became weightless and flew to heaven, left her husband dying in mortal world. her selfishness made gods very angry, they didn't allow her to live in heaven and exiled her to the moon,  a cold and lonely place，only let  a rabbit be with her.she had to stay there alone till the end of the world. so when the full moon coming in middle autumn, chinese family shall reunion and ease the missing of relatives,enjoy moon cake and the beauty of moon.elders will tell kids the story generation by generation.don't be like the selfish 嫦娥 living in a forever cold palace with no one to talk. the Osmanthus flavored wine is about another myth, a low level god（吴刚） made a mistake , he was punished to chop down a Osmanthus  tree on the moon, but every bit he chopped, the Osmanthus  tree recovered immediately, only when the tree is chopped down could he leave that cold place,  he's still chopping that tree till today, a chinese version of Sisyphus's mission. In the very early stage of Chinese civilization, the moon is symboled as a toad， the sun is symboled as a raven with three legs（三足金乌）. Hey，Martin, where  does your three-eyed raven come from?:)

this food is served in Double seven festival(七夕节). Chinese  traditional Double seven festival come from a love story: the highest ruler in heaven has 7 daughters, one day, they sneaked out and down to mortal’s living land, summer day was hot, they found a crystal clean pond and  got naked to play in the water. A  cowherd(牛郎) saw them， he was fascinated by these beautiful girls so he stole one girl's clothes and hide， those clothes happen to belong to the youngest daughter（织女），when the time was late，all goddesses need to go back to heaven secretly， but the youngest one couldn't find her clothes and started to cry（their mother is a strict goddess）,the cowherd  felt sorry for that, so he showed himself and returned  the clothes and said sorry, goddess and cowherd begin to like each other. the youngest daughter did not return to heaven, she decided to marry this cowherd, they've been living together for ten years, goddess gave birth to two sons. but goddesses' mother finally knew.(in chinese fairy tales, a day in heaven last one year in our world). She was so angry that she commanded warriors of heaven to take her daughter back. cowherd put his two sons on the back of his cow and chasing those warriors and his wife. it's almost done at the gate of heaven, goddess's mother used her hairpin drew a line in the sky between the cowherd and her  become the heaven river(now we call it milkyway), the young daughter begged her mother, her mother permitted them reunion once a year.  in every  year's Double seven festival, millions of magpies fly over the river and use their body to create a bridge, the family reunion in this day.  you can still  find a bright star（Altair） with two small stars waiting on one side, another bright star（Vega）  on the other side of the milkyway. Chinese make special food to celebrate their reunion every year.
背景音乐是《天涯明月刀LO》中的七夕主题曲《金风玉露》！
